{{neuropsychology}}
'''注意力不足過動症'''（{{lang-en|Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder}}，縮寫为{{nowrap|'''ADHD'''}}），涵蓋'''注意力缺失症'''（{{lang-en|Attention Deficit Disorder}}，縮寫为{{nowrap|'''ADD'''}}）。ADHD是一個<!--隸屬-->[[神經發展障礙|與腦神經發育相關]]的[[心理疾患|心理疾患]]<ref name="pmid23299717">{{cite journal |last1= Sroubek |first1= A |last2= Kelly |first2= M |last3= Li |first3= X | title = Inattentiveness in attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder | journal = Neuroscience Bulletin | volume = 29 | issue = 1 | pages = 103–10 | date = 2013-02 | pmid = 23299717 | doi = 10.1007/s12264-012-1295-6 | pmc=4440572}}</ref><ref name=Caroline2010>{{cite book | editor-last=Caroline | editor-first=SC | title=Encyclopedia of Cross-Cultural School Psychology | year=2010 | publisher=Springer Science & Business Media | isbn=9780387717982 | page=133 | url=https://books.google.com/books?id=PaO3jsaGkeYC&pg=PA133 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160506182307/https://books.google.com/books?id=PaO3jsaGkeYC&pg=PA133 | archivedate=2016-05-06  }}</ref>，也是一個{{tsl|en|brain disorder|中樞神經系統疾病|與腦神經相關的疾病}}<ref name="ScienceDaily 2018">{{cite web | title=Brain differences in ADHD -- ScienceDaily | website=ScienceDaily | date=2018-03-08 | url=https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2017/02/170216105919.htm | accessdate=2018-03-08 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180309120336/https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2017/02/170216105919.htm | archivedate=2018-03-09 }}</ref><ref name="Hoogman Bralten Hibar Mennes 2017 pp. 310–319 II">{{cite journal | last=Hoogman | first=Martine | last2=Bralten | first2=Janita | last3=Hibar | first3=Derrek P |last4=Mennes | first4=Maarten | last5=Zwiers | first5=Marcel P | last6=Schweren | first6=Lizanne S J 等82人| title=Subcortical brain volume differences in participants with attention deficit hyperactivity disorder in children and adults: a cross-sectional mega-analysis | journal=The lancet. Psychiatry | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=4 | issue=4 | year=2017 | issn=2215-0366 | pmid=28219628 | pmc=5933934  | doi=10.1016/s2215-0366(17)30049-4 | pages=310–319}}</ref>。它的特徵是「{{tsl|en|attentional shift|注意力轉移|容易分心，難以專注}}」、「[[#好動與過動|過度的活動]]」或「難以控制自身的言行舉止」且不符合{{tsl|en|Age appropriateness|與年齡相對應的妥適言行|患者年齡該有的成熟度}}<ref name=NIH2016/><ref name=DSM5/><!-- quote = to a degree that is inconsistent with developmental level -->。 通常患者也會有情緒管理的困難<ref>{{cite journal | vauthors = Faraone SV, Rostain AL, Blader J, Busch B, Childress AC, Connor DF, Newcorn JH | title = Practitioner Review: Emotional dysregulation in attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder - implications for clinical recognition and intervention | journal = Journal of Child Psychology and Psychiatry, and Allied Disciplines | volume = 60 | issue = 2 | pages = 133–150 | date = February 2019 | pmid = 29624671 | doi = 10.1111/jcpp.12899 }}</ref><ref>{{cite journal | vauthors = Tenenbaum RB, Musser ED, Morris S, Ward AR, Raiker JS, Coles EK, Pelham WE | title = Response Inhibition, Response Execution, and Emotion Regulation among Children with Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder | journal = Journal of Abnormal Child Psychology | volume = 47 | issue = 4 | pages = 589–603 | date = April 2019 | pmid = 30112596 | pmc = 6377355 | doi = 10.1007/s10802-018-0466-y }}</ref><ref>{{cite journal | vauthors = Lenzi F, Cortese S, Harris J, Masi G | title = Pharmacotherapy of emotional dysregulation in adults with ADHD: A systematic review and meta-analysis | journal = Neuroscience and Biobehavioral Reviews | volume = 84 | pages = 359–367 | date = January 2018 | pmid = 28837827 | doi = 10.1016/j.neubiorev.2017.08.010 }}</ref>。ADHD的症狀通常出現在大約12歲以前且持續超過六個月並在至少兩種情境中出現（例如：學校、家庭、休閒活動等）<ref name=Lake2011/><ref name=settings>{{cite web |work=Attention-Deficit / Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD) |title=Symptoms and Diagnosis |url=https://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/diagnosis.html |publisher=Division of Human Development, National Center on Birth Defects and Developmental Disabilities, Centers for Disease Control and Prevention |date=2014-09-29 |accessdate=2014-11-03 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141107202516/http://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/diagnosis.html |archivedate=2014-11-07  }}</ref><ref name=CDC>{{cite web |work=Attention-Deficit / Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD) |title=Symptoms and Diagnosis |url=https://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/diagnosis.html |publisher=Division of Human Development, National Center on Birth Defects and Developmental Disabilities, Centers for Disease Control and Prevention |date=29 September 2014 |access-date=3 November 2014 |deadurl=no |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20141107202516/http://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/diagnosis.html |archive-date=7 November 2014 }}</ref><ref name=Lake2011>{{cite book |last1= Dulcan |first1= Mina K. |last2= Lake |first2= MaryBeth | name-list-format = vanc |chapter=Axis I Disorders Usually First Diagnosed in Infancy, Childhood or Adolescence: Attention-Deficit and Disruptive Behavior Disorders |chapter-url={{google books|HvTa2nArhOsC|pages=23|plainurl=yes}} | title=Concise Guide to Child and Adolescent Psychiatry |url={{google books|HvTa2nArhOsC|plainurl=yes}} |via=Google Books | edition=4th illustrated | publisher=American Psychiatric Publishing | isbn=978-1-58562-416-4 | date=2011 | pages= [https://books.google.com/books?id=HvTa2nArhOsC&pg=PA34 34] }}</ref>。專注力方面的問題可能影響兒童患者的在學表現<ref name=NIH2016 />。除此之外，注意力不足過動症可能會導致其他心理疾病及[[物質濫用|物質濫用]]<ref>{{cite journal | vauthors = Erskine HE, Norman RE, Ferrari AJ, Chan GC, Copeland WE, Whiteford HA, Scott JG | title = Long-Term Outcomes of Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder and Conduct Disorder: A Systematic Review and Meta-Analysis | journal = Journal of the American Academy of Child and Adolescent Psychiatry | volume = 55 | issue = 10 | pages = 841–50 | date = October 2016 | pmid = 27663939 | doi = 10.1016/j.jaac.2016.06.016 }}</ref>。

<!--Epidemiology/prevalence: -->
過去普遍認為注意力不足過動症是只會發生在兒童身上的腦部發展障礙，但近年發現注意力不足過動症患者的60%（包括應接受診斷卻未接受診斷的患者），其注意力不足過動症癥狀會持續至成人時期，而這60%患者中的41%，其注意力不足過動症仍對生活造成明顯的影響<ref name="SibleySwanson2016">{{cite journal|last1=Sibley|first1=Margaret H.|last2=Swanson|first2=James M.|last3=Arnold|first3=L. Eugene|last4=Hechtman|first4=Lily T.|last5=Owens|first5=Elizabeth B.|last6=Stehli|first6=Annamarie|last7=Abikoff|first7=Howard|last8=Hinshaw|first8=Stephen P.|last9=Molina|first9=Brooke S. G.|last10=Mitchell|first10=John T.|last11=Jensen|first11=Peter S.|last12=Howard|first12=Andrea L.|last13=Lakes|first13=Kimberley D.|last14=Pelham|first14=William E.|title=Defining ADHD symptom persistence in adulthood: optimizing sensitivity and specificity|journal=Journal of Child Psychology and Psychiatry|year=2016|issn=00219630|doi=10.1111/jcpp.12620}}</ref><ref name="II">{{Cite journal
| author = Margaret H. Sibley, James M. Swanson, L. Eugene Arnold, Lily T. Hechtman, Elizabeth B. Owens, Annamarie Stehli, Howard Abikoff, Stephen P. Hinshaw, Brooke S. G. Molina, John T. Mitchell, Peter S. Jensen, Andrea L. Howard, Kimberley D. Lakes & William E. Pelham
 | title = Defining ADHD symptom persistence in adulthood: optimizing sensitivity and specificity
 | journal = Journal of child psychology and psychiatry, and allied disciplines
 | doi = 10.1111/jcpp.12620
 | pmid = 27642116
 |quote=CONCLUSION:The interview format optimizes young adult self-reporting when parent reports are not available. However, the combination of parent and self-reports from rating scales, using an 'or' rule and a NB threshold optimized the balance between sensitivity and specificity. With this definition, 60% of the ADHD group demonstrated symptom persistence and 41% met both symptom and impairment criteria in adulthood.
| date= 2016-09}}</ref><ref name="III">{{cite web
 |url         = https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/topics/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-adhd/index.shtml
 |title       = Signs and symptoms of Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder, National Institute of Mental Health.
 |date        = 2013-03
 |website     = nimh.nih.gov
 |publisher   = National Institute of mental health
 |language    = en
 |accessdate = 2017-01
 |quote       = Many adolescents with ADHD also struggle with relationships and antisocial behaviors. Inattention, restlessness, and impulsivity tend to persist into adulthood. Symptoms of ADHD can be mistaken for emotional or disciplinary problems or missed entirely in quiet, well-behaved children, leading to a delay in diagnosis. Adults with undiagnosed ADHD may have a history of poor academic performance, problems at work, or difficult or failed relationships.
 |deadurl     = no
 |archiveurl  = https://web.archive.org/web/20161229084207/https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/topics/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-adhd/index.shtml
 |archivedate = 2016-12-29
}}</ref><ref name="衛生福利部 注意力不足過動症">{{cite book
 | author = 蔣丙煌
 | author2 =陳快樂
 | author3 = 國立臺灣大學醫學院附設醫院精神醫學部
 | author4 =張雍敏、鄭淑心、賴淑玲、傅悅娟、張景瑞、侯育銘、郭約瑟、張君威、鄧惠文、陳嘉新、紀雪雲、黃雅文、連玉如、連盈如、吳其炘
 | author5 =高淑芬&陳劭芊
 | title = 注意力不足過動症
 | publisher = 中華民國衛生福利部
 | series = 衛生福利部精神疾病衛教叢書
 | volume = 02
 | edition = First
 | location = Taipei
 | language = zh-tw
 | date = 2015-06
 | doi = 
 | isbn = 9789860454154
 | url =https://www.mohw.gov.tw/dl-1728-547a9d89-00e5-4e9e-b998-26cff0ee69e7.html
 | archiveurl =https://web.archive.org/web/20170219181830/http://www.mohw.gov.tw/MOHW_Upload/doc/%E5%BF%83%E7%90%86%E8%A1%9B%E7%94%9F%E5%B0%88%E8%BC%AF/03%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%8D%E8%B6%B3%E9%81%8E%E5%8B%95%E7%97%87.pdf
 | archivedate =2017-02-19
 | page = 19-20
 | quote=藉由成人 ADHD 的回顧性研究或是長期追蹤研究可發現，孩童時期的 ADHD 患者，在成年後僅有2成左右的人完全沒有症狀、另外有2成有輕微不致干擾的症狀，其餘近6成的人雖然症狀較孩童時期有所減輕，但仍達到生活顯著困擾程度。不只是ADHD的核心症狀，許多次發症狀或是共病，並不會隨著年紀增長而減少或是消失，甚至產生長久的負面影響（物質濫用依賴、慢性焦慮憂鬱等）。除了再度說明 ADHD 是一個長期慢性的神經發展疾病以外，也讓我們發現，如果早期了解 ADHD，給予合適的治療介入時，孩童長期的預後將會大有不同。}}</ref>。注意力不足過動症在嬰兒和幼兒時期，因為孩子正在學走路和說話，所以症狀通常不易被察覺，往往要等到他們進入幼稚園或小學之後，透過遵守教室、課堂的規範及跟同學們的相處，旁人才會漸漸注意到其症狀。學校老師往往是最容易發現孩童注意力不足過動症症狀的人，因為在學校有明確的[[對照組|對照組]]<ref name=Erk2009>{{cite book |vauthors=Mayes R, Bagwell C, Erkulwater JL | title=Medicating Children: ADHD and Pediatric Mental Health | publisher=Harvard University Press | date=2009 | pages=4–24 | isbn=9780674031630 | edition=illustrated }}</ref>；然而，不少注意力不足過動症患者（尤其是女性患者）沒有過動—衝動的症狀，而過去對此症的認識總是集中在過動{{efn|即多動、過度活躍}}症狀上，使得這類「不[[#好動與過動|過動]]或[[#衝動性|衝動]]」、「純粹[[#注意力不足（失調/缺陷）|注意力缺陷]]」的注意力不足過動症患者甚少能診斷出來。端視注意力不足過動症患者其腦部發展的程度與其所在環境對其執行功能要求的程度之比例，因此有些注意力不足過動症患者可能直到青少年時期甚至是成年期（特別是成年初期）才開始顯露出注意力不足過動症的症狀<ref name="Brown-2008">{{cite journal | vauthors = Brown TE | title = ADD/ADHD and Impaired Executive Function in Clinical Practice | journal = Current Psychiatry Reports | volume = 10 | issue = 5 | pages = 407–11 | date = October 2008 | pmid = 18803914 | doi = 10.1007/s11920-008-0065-7 }}</ref><ref name="Tc_ADHD" /><ref name="UpToDate 2016 on adults with ADHD">{{cite web | title=Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder in adults: Epidemiology, pathogenesis, clinical features, course, assessment, and diagnosis | website=[[UpToDate|UpToDate]] | date=2016-11-03 | url=https://www.uptodate.com/contents/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-in-adults-epidemiology-pathogenesis-clinical-features-course-assessment-and-diagnosis | accessdate=2017-10-29 | quote=Some adults present with impairment in a clinical setting only later in life when they confront new and increasingly complex tasks that characterize adulthood and that cannot be managed with their existing neuropsychological repertoire. | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171030003257/https://www.uptodate.com/contents/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-in-adults-epidemiology-pathogenesis-clinical-features-course-assessment-and-diagnosis | archivedate=2017-10-30 }}</ref><ref name="Canela Buadze Dube Eich 2017 p=e0184964">{{cite journal | last=Canela | first=Carlos | last2=Buadze | first2=Anna | last3=Dube | first3=Anish | last4=Eich | first4=Dominique | last5=Liebrenz | first5=Michael | editor-last=Chao | editor-first=Linda | title=Skills and compensation strategies in adult ADHD – A qualitative study | journal=PloS one | publisher=Public Library of Science (PLoS) | volume=12 | issue=9 | date=2017-09-27 | issn=1932-6203 | pmid=28953946 | pmc=5617155 | doi=10.1371/journal.pone.0184964 | page=e0184964}}</ref>。國際注意力不足過動症，兒童[[流行率|流行率]]中位數為5~8%<ref name="Thomas Sanders Doust Beller 2015 pp. e994–e1001"/>，成人流行率為2.5~5%<ref name="underdiagnosed">{{cite journal | vauthors = Ginsberg Y, Quintero J, Anand E, Casillas M, Upadhyaya HP | title = Underdiagnosis of attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder in adult patients: a review of the literature | journal = The Primary Care Companion for CNS Disorders | volume = 16 | issue = 3 | year = 2014 | pmid = 25317367 | pmc = 4195639 | doi = 10.4088/PCC.13r01600 | quote = Reports indicate that ADHD affects 2.5%–5% of adults in the general population,<sup>5–8</sup> compared with 5%–7% of children.<sup>9,10</sup> ... However, fewer than 20% of adults with ADHD are currently diagnosed and/or treated by psychiatrists.<sup>7,15,16</sup> }}</ref>。注意力不足過動症會造成家庭社會的重大損失，其中也包括父母的工作損失<ref name="ScienceDirect 2015 pp. 42–58">{{cite web | title=Attention Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder | website=ScienceDirect | date=2015-01-01 | doi=10.1016/B978-0-12-398270-4.00004-5 | url=https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/B9780123982704000045 | access-date=2018-09-19 | pages=42–58 | quote=ADHD imposes an enormous burden on society in terms of psychological dysfunction, adverse vocational outcomes, stress on families, and societal financial costs. The US annual incremental costs of ADHD have been estimated at 143–266 billion USD.}}</ref><ref name="outcomes with untreated ADHD">
{{cite web| title =【誤解下的小孩】：談注意力不足/過動症 - 陳錦宏醫師| url =http://www.tc-adhd.com/?p=147| website =社團法人台灣心動家族兒童青少年關懷協會| accessdate =2017-02-16| date =2012-07-09| author =陳錦宏| deadurl =no| archiveurl =https://web.archive.org/web/20180224050902/http://www.tc-adhd.com/?p=147| archivedate =2018-02-24}}</ref>。注意力不足過動症患者甚至其家屬可能對自身或患者的問題存有[[否認心理|否認心理]]<ref name="I">{{cite web
 |url          = https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2016/10/161020132300.htm
 |title        = ADHD symptom persistence into adulthood estimated
 |date         = 2016-10-20
 |website      = Science News
 |publisher    = Journal of Child Psychology and Psychiatry, 2016
 |language     = en
 |deadurl      = no
 |accessdate   = 2017-01-01
 |archiveurl   = https://web.archive.org/web/20170102050323/https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2016/08/160801093232.htm
 |archivedate  = 2017-01-02
}}</ref><ref>高淑芬 2016. 找回專注力：成人ADHD全方位自助手冊. 心靈工坊, 台北. "成人ADHD的診斷"章節</ref><ref name="Barkley 2013 Taking charge of ADHD : the complete, authoritative guide for parents">{{cite book | last=Barkley | first=Russell | title=Taking charge of ADHD : the complete, authoritative guide for parents | publisher=The Guilford Press | publication-place=New York | year=2013 | isbn=978-1-4625-0789-4 | oclc=825196454 | page=152-153}}</ref>。

<!--Diagnosis:-->
現時沒有任何確切證據證實任何一個或多個因素決定性地導致這種病症。研究顯示注意力不足過動症與腦部的[[額葉|額葉]]及其他構造發展相關，但詳細成因仍未得知。注意力不足過動症可能具有相當高的[[遺傳率|遺傳率]]。根據[[美国疾病控制与预防中心|美国疾病控制与预防中心]]的研究，注意力不足過動症是一群症狀的交集。因此，要正確診斷這病症，不能依靠單一臨床方法去確定，而必須同時採用多種臨床方法配合去確認。注意力不足過動症的診斷係依據《[[精神疾病診斷與統計手冊|精神疾病診斷與統計手冊]]》的標準、門診病人[[主訴|主訴]]<!-- 對自身病情的描述 -->、症狀學、患者的歷史經歷、發展史、家族史、{{link-en|共病|Comorbidity}}、[[生理評估|生理評估]]及各種醫師評估後認為需要進一步的檢查等。{{noteTag|name=developmentally|1=心理測驗只是進一步進行各種測驗的選項之一，非必要選項。}}<ref name="CDC 2017 How US children are diagnosed with ADHD
">{{cite web | author=CDC | title=How US children are diagnosed with ADHD | website=Centers for Disease Control and Prevention | date=2017-09-08 | url=https://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/features/how-us-children-diagnosed.html | accessdate=2018-07-15}}</ref><ref name="NIMH » Home">{{cite web | title=NIMH » Could I Have Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD)? | website=NIMH » Home | url=https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/publications/could-i-have-adhd/index.shtml | accessdate=2018-07-13 | quote=There is no one test that can diagnose ADHD. Mental health professionals use certain rating scales to determine if an adult meets the diagnostic criteria for ADHD. A thorough evaluation also includes looking at the person’s history of childhood behavior and school experiences. To obtain this information, the doctor may interview spouses or partners, parents, close friends, and other associates. The person may also undergo a physical exam and various psychological tests that evaluate working memory, executive functioning (abilities like planning and decision-making), and visual and spatial skills or reasoning. The evaluation will also look at the person’s mood and whether he or she struggles with other issues, such as anxiety, depression, or substance abuse. A person’s medical history is also important, as previous health problems, trauma, or injury can also be the cause of symptoms. | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180601233900/https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/publications/could-i-have-adhd/index.shtml | archivedate=2018-06-01 }}</ref><ref name="Tc_ADHD">{{cite web| url =http://www.tc-adhd.com/?p=1850#more-1850| title =心動家族:注意力不足過動症ＡＤＨＤ的第三條路| date =2016-12-13| website =台灣心動家族兒童青少年關懷協會| publisher =Tc-adhd.com| language =zh-tw| accessdate =2017-02| author =陳錦宏 | deadurl =no| archiveurl =https://web.archive.org/web/20180224050902/http://www.tc-adhd.com/?p=1850#more-1850| archivedate =2018-02-24}}</ref>每年的十月為國際間訂定的注意力不足過動症意識之月（ADHD Awareness Month）<ref name="ADHD awareness month"/><ref name="Healthline 2018 Awareness periods"/>。

<!--治療及預後-->
每個國家都有各自的[[ADHD的治療|ADHD治療策略]]，彼此之間並不完全相同，但大都包含[[心理治療|諮商]]、改變生活習慣和藥物等。<ref name="NIH2016"/>。學齡前的患者，通常僅需接受行為治療，除非症狀達到嚴重的程度且拒絕接受行為治療或無法從行為治療中獲得改善，才需考慮加入藥物治療<ref name="Guidelines_May_Have_Helped_Curb_ADHD_Diagnoses_in_Preschoolers"/><ref name="behavior treatment for ADHD from the CDC">
{{cite web
 |website     = Central for Disease Control, United States of America.
 |title       = Behavior therapy for young children with ADHD
 |url         = https://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/behavior-therapy.html
 |date        = 2017-04-10
 |accessdate  = 2017-04-12
 |deadurl     = no
 |archiveurl  = https://web.archive.org/web/20170413071307/https://www.cdc.gov/ncbddd/adhd/behavior-therapy.html
 |archivedate = 2017-04-13
}}</ref>。中樞神經刺激劑是最常用的ADHD藥物，使用者在頭14個月持續服用能有效治療ADHD，不過目前有關使用超過14個月後對於ADHD症狀的療效，尚未明朗。<ref name="NICE 2009"/><ref name="Long-Term Outcomes Medications">{{cite journal | vauthors = Huang YS, Tsai MH | title = Long-term outcomes with medications for attention-deficit hyperactivity disorder: current status of knowledge | journal = CNS Drugs | volume = 25 | issue = 7 | pages = 539–54 | date = July 2011 | pmid = 21699268 | doi = 10.2165/11589380-000000000-00000 }}</ref><ref name="Long-term 2015">{{cite journal | vauthors = Arnold LE, Hodgkins P, Caci H, Kahle J, Young S | title = Effect of treatment modality on long-term outcomes in attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder: a systematic review | journal = PLOS One | volume = 10 | issue = 2 | pages = e0116407 | date = February 2015 | pmid = 25714373 | pmc = 4340791 | doi = 10.1371/journal.pone.0116407 | displayauthors = 4 }}</ref><ref name="Long-term 36">{{cite journal | vauthors = Parker J, Wales G, Chalhoub N, Harpin V | title = The long-term outcomes of interventions for the management of attention-deficit hyperactivity disorder in children and adolescents: a systematic review of randomized controlled trials | journal = Psychology Research and Behavior Management | volume = 6 | issue =  | pages = 87–99 | date = September 2013 | pmid = 24082796 | pmc = 3785407 | doi = 10.2147/PRBM.S49114 | quote = Results suggest there is moderate-to-high-level evidence that combined pharmacological and behavioral interventions, and pharmacological interventions alone can be effective in managing the core ADHD symptoms and academic performance at 14 months. However, the effect size may decrease beyond this period. ... Only one paper examining outcomes beyond 36 months met the review criteria. ... There is high level evidence suggesting that pharmacological treatment can have a major beneficial effect on the core symptoms of ADHD (hyperactivity, inattention, and impulsivity) in approximately 80% of cases compared with placebo controls, in the short term.22 }}</ref>。成人患者多半會發展出應對的技巧，來處理其部份或是所有的不足之處<ref name="Art.218"/>。

<!--當前之環境與方向-->
雖然中樞神經刺激劑不會帶給服用者嚴重的副作用，但其相對不嚴重的副作用，比如說：失眠、食慾不振則較常出現在服用者身上。對於「如何解決前述的副作用」和「非藥物的治療方式」是未來研究的重點<ref name="Storebø Ramstad Krogh Nilausen p. II "/>。注意力不足過動症的治療並非是要將孩子們標準化{{efn|即為一致化}}，而是一本教育的初衷，協助每一位孩子「發掘、發揚自己的優點、並避免缺點」。<ref name="找回專注力">{{cite book|author=[[高淑芬|高淑芬]] |title=找回專注力：成人ADHD全方位自助手冊 |publisher=心靈工坊|language =zh-tw|location=台北 |isbn=9789863570592 |date=2016-05-09 |accessdate=2016-12-12|url=http://books.google.com/books?id=0h8qnQAACAAJ }}</ref><ref name="幫助ADHD孩子快樂成長"/><ref name="books2000"/><ref name="分心也有好成績">{{cite book|url=http://books.google.com/books?id=NEyiGQAACAAJ|author1=Edward M. Hallowell, M.D.|author2=John J. Ratey, M.D.|others=丁凡譯|title=《分心也有好成績》，| location =台北|year=2006 |publisher=遠流出版社 |isbn=9573259311 |date= |accessdate=2016-12-09}}</ref>

<!--History, society and culture -->
18世紀首次有人在醫學文獻上描述類似當今ADHD定義的症狀。<ref name="Lange Reichl 2010">{{cite journal | vauthors = Lange KW, Reichl S, Lange KM, Tucha L, Tucha O | title = The history of attention deficit hyperactivity disorder | journal = Attention Deficit and Hyperactivity Disorders | volume = 2 | issue = 4 | pages = 241–55 | date = December 2010 | pmid = 21258430 | pmc = 3000907 | doi = 10.1007/s12402-010-0045-8 | doi-access=free }}</ref> 近年來，ADHD本身和ADHD診斷以及ADHD治療時常[[ADHD的爭議|引發爭議]]。<ref name="Parrillo 2008 63">{{Cite book | title=Encyclopedia of Social Problems | vauthors = Parrillo VN | year=2008 | publisher=SAGE | isbn=9781412941655 | pages=63 | url=https://books.google.com/?id=mRGr_B4Y1CEC | access-date=2 May 2009 }}</ref> 圍繞在爭議中的當事人包含醫師、教師、政府官員（政策制定者）、父母和新聞媒體，他們主要在爭論「ADHD的起因」和「使用中樞神經刺激藥物來治療ADHD是否合適」。<ref name=May2008>{{cite journal | vauthors = Mayes R, Bagwell C, Erkulwater J | title = ADHD and the rise in stimulant use among children | journal = Harvard Review of Psychiatry | volume = 16 | issue = 3 | pages = 151–66 | date = 2008 | pmid = 18569037 | doi = 10.1080/10673220802167782 }}</ref>
大多數的醫療從業人員都接受ADHD是一個真實存在的疾病且見於兒童、青少年和成人，存在於這些醫療人士之間的歧見肇因於對「ADHD的診斷方式」、「ADHD的治療方式」和「[[精神科醫師|精神科醫師]]應具備的專業素養」的不同看法<ref name="Sim">{{cite journal | vauthors = Sim MG, Hulse G, Khong E | title = When the child with ADHD grows up | journal = Australian Family Physician | volume = 33 | issue = 8 | pages = 615–8 | date = August 2004 | pmid = 15373378 | doi =  | url = http://www.racgp.org.au/afp/200408/20040803sim.pdf | format = PDF | archive-url = https://web.archive.org/web/20150924083931/http://www.racgp.org.au/afp/200408/20040803sim.pdf | df = dmy-all | deadurl = no | archive-date = 24 September 2015 }}</ref><ref name="Online">{{cite book| vauthors = Silver LB |title=Attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder | publisher=American Psychiatric Publishing | edition=3rd | year=2004 | isbn=978-1-58562-131-6 | pages=4–7 }}</ref><ref name="Schonwald">{{cite journal | vauthors = Schonwald A, Lechner E | title = Attention deficit/hyperactivity disorder: complexities and controversies | journal = Current Opinion in Pediatrics | volume = 18 | issue = 2 | pages = 189–95 | date = April 2006 | pmid = 16601502 | doi = 10.1097/01.mop.0000193302.70882.70 }}</ref><ref name="patients' second abused experience"/><ref name="lacking professional training"/>。 ADHD在早期的官方稱呼為'''注意力缺失症'''（{{lang-en|attention-deficit disorder、ADD}}）和'''兒童過度活躍的反應'''（{{lang-en|hyperkinetic reaction of childhood}}）<ref name=We2005>{{cite book|last1=Weiss|first1=Lawrence G.| name-list-format = vanc |title=WISC-IV clinical use and interpretation scientist-practitioner perspectives|date=2005|publisher=Elsevier Academic Press|location=Amsterdam|isbn=978-0-12-564931-5|pages=237|edition=1st|url=https://books.google.com/books?id=Eg9U9e_ICr8C&pg=PA237 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news|title=ADHD: The Diagnostic Criteria|url=https://www.pbs.org/wgbh/pages/frontline/shows/medicating/adhd/diagnostic.html|access-date=5 March 2016|agency=Frontline|publisher=PBS|deadurl=no|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20160420080026/http://www.pbs.org/wgbh/pages/frontline/shows/medicating/adhd/diagnostic.html|archive-date=20 April 2016}}</ref>。

== 名稱 ==

'''注意力不足過動症'''也译作'''注意力不集中/過動症'''（{{lang-en|Attention Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder}}，簡稱{{nowrap|'''AD/HD'''}}）、'''過度活躍症'''（{{lang-en|Hyperkinetic Disorder}}；於[[國際疾病傷害及死因分類標準第十版|ICD 10]]中的名稱），俗称有'''多動症'''、'''多動障礙'''及'''[[大雄·胖虎症候群|大雄·胖虎症候群]]'''（日本）等。此病患的兒童習稱'''過動兒'''，也有醫療人士建議改稱為'''心動兒'''。<ref name="IV">{{cite web|url=http://www.tc-adhd.com/?page_id=957|title=台灣心動家族兒童青少年關懷協會理事長陳錦宏醫師 敬上|author=陳錦宏|publisher=Tc-adhd.com|language=zh-tw|date=2015-04-18|accessdate=2016-12-09|quote=理事長的話：在這場演講，協會提出第一個主張，我們主張將ADHD原本「過動兒」的中文稱呼改為「心動兒」，因為ADHD包含沒有過動症狀的不專心兒童，「過動兒」常令人混淆，另外過動兒文字本身即包含負面意涵，而心動兒無此字義上的問題。|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180224050902/http://www.tc-adhd.com/?page_id=957|archivedate=2018-02-24}}</ref><ref name="WWW.COMMONHEALW 2017">{{cite web| title=過動兒現象如何避免被以偏概全| website=[[康健雜誌|康健雜誌]]| date=2017-01-25| url=//m.commonhealth.com.tw/article/article.action?nid=72375| language=zh| author=陳錦宏| accessdate=2018-04-14| archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170924045255/https://m.commonhealth.com.tw/article/article.action?nid=72375| archivedate=2017-09-24}}</ref>

注意力不足過動症可以依其子類型分為以下幾類。
<!-- 通常而言，注意力不足過動症意指包含過動（多動、過度活躍）症狀在內的所有注意力不足過動症類型，包含注意力缺失症-->

|style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|過動-衝動為主型{{noteTag|name=|1=「過動」與「衝動」相連是因為兩者高度相關<ref name="BARKLEY 1989 pp. 203–233">{{cite book | last=BARKLEY | first=RUSSELL A. | title=Current Concepts and Emerging Trends in Attentional and Behavioral Disorders of Childhood | chapter=THE PROBLEM OF STIMULUS CONTROL AND RULE-GOVERNED BEHAVIOR IN ATTENTION DEFICIT DISORDER WITH HYPERACTIVITY | publisher=Elsevier | year=1989 | isbn=978-0-08-036508-4 | doi=10.1016/b978-0-08-036508-4.50017-5 | pages=203–233}}</ref>。}} || - || ✔ || ✔

[[世界衛生組織|世界衛生組織]]出版的《[[世界通用疾病分類手冊|世界通用疾病分類手冊]]》第十版中（ICD-10, International Classification of Disease-10，又稱為國際通用的疾病分類表）， 過度活躍症的症狀幾乎等同於《精神疾病診斷與統計手冊》第五版（DSM-5）中注意力不足過動症的症狀。而「注意力不足過動症」在ICD-10中稱為「過度活躍症」<ref name=ICD10>{{citation | title=International Statistical Classification of Diseases and Related Health Problems 10th Revision | year=2010 | publisher=World Health Organisation | accessdate=2014-11-02 | url=http://apps.who.int/classifications/icd10/browse/2010/en#/F90 | chapter=F90 Hyperkinetic disorders | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20141102133725/http://apps.who.int/classifications/icd10/browse/2010/en#/F90 | archivedate=2014-11-02 }}</ref>。

ICD-11 正式版將廢除「過度活躍症」名稱，改採「注意力不足/過動症」<ref name="ICD-11 reference to ADHD">{{cite web | title=Mortality and Morbidity Statistics | website=ICD-11 | archive-url=https://archive.is/W49AD | archive-date=2018-10-3 | url=https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f294762853 | access-date=2018-09-25}}</ref>並納入上述三種ADHD的類型、子類型<ref name="ICD-11  predominantly inattentive presentation
">{{cite web | title=6A05.0 Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder, predominantly inattentive presentation | archive-url=https://archive.today/20180801205234/https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en%23/http://id.who.int/icd/entity/294762853#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f294762853 | archive-date=2018-08-01 | website=ICD-11 | url=https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f294762853 | access-date=2018-07-21 | quote=Inattention refers to significant difficulty in sustaining attention to tasks that do not provide a high level of stimulation or frequent rewards, distractibility and problems with organization. | dead-url=no }}</ref><ref name="ICD-11 6A05.1 Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder, predominantly hyperactive-impulsive presentation">{{cite web | archive-url=https://archive.today/20180801205500/https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en%23/http://id.who.int/icd/entity/209556851#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f209556851 | archive-date=2018-08-01 | title=6A05.1 Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder, predominantly hyperactive-impulsive presentation | website=ICD-11 | url=https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f209556851 | access-date=2018-07-21 | dead-url=no }}</ref><ref name="ICD-11 6A05.2 Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder, combined presentation">{{cite web | title=Mortality and Morbidity Statistics | website=ICD-11 | url=https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f542202013 | access-date=2018-07-21 | quote=6A05.2 Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder, combined presentation | archive-url=https://archive.today/20180801205735/https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en%23/http://id.who.int/icd/entity/542202013#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f542202013 | archive-date=2018-08-01 | dead-url=no }}</ref>。

== 定義 ==

[[File:Attention_deficit_hyperactivity_disorder_video.webm|upright=1.4]]

對注意力不足過動症比較確切的定義，記載於[[美國精神醫學會|美國精神醫學會]]（APA）出版的《[[精神疾病診斷與統計手冊|精神疾病診斷與統計手冊]]》（DSM）第四版之文本修改版<ref name="Association2000">{{cite book|author=American Psychiatric Association|title=Diagnostic and Statistical Manual of Mental Disorders, Fourth Edition: DSM-IV-TR®|url=https://books.google.com/books?id=3SQrtpnHb9MC|year=2000|publisher=American Psychiatric Association|isbn=978-0-89042-025-6|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160512190609/https://books.google.com/books?id=3SQrtpnHb9MC|archivedate=2016-05-12}}</ref>。

注意力不足過動症的主要病徵是：

# 注意力渙散或集中困難（專注力失調、注意力缺陷）
# 活動量過多 （過度活躍、多動）
# [[自我管理|自我管理]]能力弱 （[[衝動_(心理學)|衝動]]）

基於以上三種病徵，再把注意力不足過動症細分為以下三個分類：

# 注意力渙散主導型<br/>又稱為注意力不足（專注力失調）為主型
# 活動量過多或自制力弱主導型<br/>又稱為過動-衝動（過度活躍、多動障礙）為主型
# 混合型<br/>又稱為注意力不足（專注力失調）、過動-衝動（過度活躍、多動障礙）混和型

=== 注意力不足（失調/缺陷） ===
      參見：[[注意#注意力的臨床表現型|注意力的臨床表現型]]、[[注意力不集中|注意力不集中]]、[[分心|分心]]、[[過度專心|過度專心]]

{| class="wikitable sortable"
|-
! style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|面向 !! style="background:#ffe5f6;" colspan="1"|解釋
|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|選擇性注意力<br/> （Selective attention）||

#能夠維持原有的行為或認知過程，即便遇到外界的刺激或誘惑，亦复如此。
#能夠將注意力凝聚於某一個重要[[目標|目標]]，而忽略其他不相干的訊息，所以就不會分心。

|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|分開性注意力<br/> （Divided attention）||

能夠同時專注於不同的事情上、同時接收多個指令、或者同時進行好幾件事情而不會搞混或忘記。
|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|轉移性注意力<br/>（Shifting/Alternating attention）||

#專注力可以迅速從一件事切換到另一件事，果斷地處理完眼前的事物、再隨時切換回去，不會遲疑不決或慌張混亂。
#能夠在心靈上保有彈性，使自己能把注意力的焦點從一件事切換到另一件事，也能在「所需認知程度不同的」事情之間切換。
|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|持續的[[注意的長度|注意]]<nowiki>/</nowiki>{{tsl|en|Vigilance (psychology)|警覺 (心理學)|警覺}}<nowiki>/</nowiki>[[專注|專注]]力<br/>（Sustained Attention/Vigilance/ Concentration）
||
可以讓專注力在「持續一段時間且內容重複」的事情中保持一段較長的時間，不會一下子就恍神或散漫。
|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|集中的注意力（選擇地集中注意力）<br/>（Focused attention/Selective sustained attention<ref>{{cite journal|last1=Wilson|first1=Karen|last2=Korn|first2=James H.|title=Attention During Lectures: Beyond Ten Minutes|journal=Teaching of Psychology|date=2007-06-05|volume=34|issue=2|pages=85–89|doi=10.1080/00986280701291291}}</ref><ref name=Essential>{{cite book |first2=Dianne |last2=Dukette |first1=David |last1=Cornish |title=The Essential 20: Twenty Components of an Excellent Health Care Team |location=Pittsburgh, PA |publisher=RoseDog Books |year=2009 |pages=72–73 |oclc=721335045 |isbn=1-4349-9555-0}}</ref>）||

能夠一個一個，井然有序地應對來自[[視覺|視覺]]、[[聽覺|聽覺]]或[[觸覺|觸覺]]等外部刺激。
|}

[[File:Confused_Felipe.jpg|thumb]]

* 備註：「一件事」在此也可為「一個想法或[[點子_(心理)|點子]]」。

注意力不足過動症的兒童，在「轉移性注意力」、「選擇性注意力」和「持續性注意力」有類似的特點，尤其是「持續性注意力」，會低於同年齡無ADHD的兒童<ref>{{cite web |url=http://www.ntcu.edu.tw/spc/aspc/6_ebook/pdf/9301/1.pdf |language=zh |title=ADHD兒童的注意力特質及其相關研究 |publisher=國立台中教育大學 特殊教育中心 |author=王乙婷 |accessdate=2017-10-07 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160528022926/http://www.ntcu.edu.tw/spc/aspc/6_ebook/pdf/9301/1.pdf |archivedate=2016-05-28 }}</ref>。
父母常疑問：孩子在看電視或打電動時常常一坐就是幾小時，可是靜態的[[看書|看書]]、[[畫畫|畫畫]]就沒有辦法，可能幾分鐘就喊無聊。不過不同活動所需的專注度原本就有差異，[[電視|電視]]與[[电子游戏|電動]]因為畫面不停的變換，加上各種[[聽覺效果|聽覺效果]]、[[視覺效果|視覺吸引的效果]]（包含時下興起的：[[虛擬實境|虛擬實境]]），只需維持短暫的注意力就能持續進行，但孩子一旦從事要求較長專注度的工作或是活動時，其注意力就會無法持續或出現缺失。<ref name="找回專注力" /><ref name="幫助ADHD孩子快樂成長" /><ref name="衛生福利部 注意力不足過動症 p.19-20">衛生福利部精神疾病衛教叢書 注意力不足過動症，第19至20頁</ref><ref name="Mangal1995">{{cite book|author=S.K. Mangal|title=An Introduction To Psychology|url=https://books.google.com/books?id=wVVp7f7fRzMC&pg=PR8|year=1995|publisher=Sterling Publishers Pvt. Ltd|isbn=978-81-207-1840-1|pages=8, 69|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180224050902/https://books.google.com/books?id=wVVp7f7fRzMC&pg=PR8|archivedate=2018-02-24}}</ref>而許多ADHD的孩子在自身感興趣的事情上可以維持長時間的專注<ref name="Tc_ADHD"/><ref name="pmid22851461">{{cite journal |last1= Walitza |first1= S |last2= Drechsler |first2= R |last3= Ball |first3= J |trans-title=The school child with ADHD |title= Das schulkind mit ADHS |language= DE |journal=Ther Umsch |volume=69 |issue=8 |pages=467–73 |date=August 2012 |pmid=22851461 |doi=10.1024/0040-5930/a000316 }}</ref>。

簡而言之，「注意力不足/缺陷」指的就是難以把注意力維持在「沒有帶給個案高強度{{tsl|en|Stimulus_(psychology)|刺激 (心理學)|刺激感}}或沒有頻繁帶給個案{{tsl|en|reward||獎賞、回饋、或滿足感}}（Reward）」的事情上或容易分心且有組織規劃上的困難。<ref name="ICD-11  predominantly inattentive presentation"/>

{{-}}

===好動與過動===

{{see also2|{{tsl|en|Hyperkinesia|過動的病理學}}}}

[[File:Tapping_pencil.jpg|thumb]]

{| class="wikitable"
|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|'''好動''' || 雖然活動量大，但是「神經動作」、「精細動作」的控制沒有問題，是故可以進行靜態的活動。<ref name="衛生福利部 注意力不足過動症"/>{{RP|19-20}}
|-
| style="background:honeyDew;" colspan="1"|'''過動''' || 過動者在靜止時容易有主觀的「不安」感覺。若患者不被允許進行大動作（走路、站立）時，其會需要透過小幅度的動作（如抖腳、[[轉筆|轉筆]]等）來化解坐立不安的感覺。<ref name="衛生福利部 注意力不足過動症 p.19-20"/><ref name="healthdirect 2017">{{cite web | title=Overactive children and ADHD | website=healthdirect | date=2017-03-09 | url=https://www.healthdirect.gov.au/overactive-children-and-adhd | accessdate=2017-07-07 | quote= | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171006211502/https://www.healthdirect.gov.au/overactive-children-and-adhd | archivedate=2017-10-06 }}</ref><ref name="MedlinePlus 2018">{{cite web | title=Hyperactivity and children: MedlinePlus Medical Encyclopedia | website=MedlinePlus | date=2018-06-04 | url=https://medlineplus.gov/ency/article/001984.htm | accessdate=2018-06-14 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171223020602/https://medlineplus.gov/ency/article/001984.htm | archivedate=2017-12-23 }}</ref>
除此之外，過動的孩子往往無時無刻都保持動態，難以維持肢體上的固定（在那些需要自我控制肢體的場合中動來動去就是證據之一）；也會顯得過於活躍、[[侵略_(社會科學)|帶有攻擊性]]、[[衝動_(心理學)|衝動]]或難以保持專注，並造成社交上和學業上的困難。<ref name="MedlinePlus 2018"/><ref name="MedlinePlus 2017 Hyperactive or just active or energetic">{{cite web | title=Hyperactivity: MedlinePlus Medical Encyclopedia | website=MedlinePlus | date=2017-07-05 | url=https://medlineplus.gov/ency/article/003256.htm | accessdate=2017-07-07| type=tertiary source | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170715025355/https://medlineplus.gov/ency/article/003256.htm | archivedate=2017-07-15| quote=Hyperactivity means having increased movement, impulsive actions, and a shorter attention span, and being easily distracted...... Hyperactivity is not easily defined. It often depends on the observer. Behavior that seems excessive to one person may not seem excessive to another. But certain children, when compared to others, are clearly far more active. This can become a problem if it interferes with school work or making friends.}}</ref><ref name="ICD-11">{{cite web | title=Mortality and Morbidity Statistics | website=ICD-11 | url=https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f821852937 | quote=Hyperactivity refers to excessive motor activity and difficulties with remaining still, most evident in structured situations that require behavioural self-control. | accessdate=2018-06-23 | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180623134621/https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f821852937 | archivedate=2018-06-23 | deadurl=no }}</ref><ref name="Lipkin Mostofsky 2007 pp. 631–639">{{cite book | last=Lipkin | first=Paul H. | last2=Mostofsky | first2=Stewart | title=Neurobiology of Disease | chapter=Attention-Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder | publisher=Elsevier | year=2007 | isbn=978-0-12-088592-3 | doi=10.1016/b978-012088592-3/50059-1 | pages=631–639}}</ref>{{NoteTag|name=coordinatate}}

從青春期開始直到往後的人生，過動-衝動的症狀往往不再明顯以外部的肢體表現出來，而是轉為以「內在的不安寧（inner restlessness）」等內在型式表現。
<ref name="Anas2001">{{cite book|last1=Anastopoulos|first1=Arthur D.|last2=Shelton|first2=Terri L.|title=Assessing attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder|series=Topics in Social Psychiatry|date=2001-05-31|publisher=Kluwer Academic/Plenum Publishers|location=New York|isbn=978-0-306-46388-4|oclc=51784126}}</ref><ref>{{cite book |last=Hechtman|first=Lily |chapter=ADHD in Adults|date=2009-02-08|title=ADHD Comorbidities: Handbook for ADHD Complications in Children and Adults|edition=1st|editor-last=Brown|editor-first=Thomas E.|publisher=American Psychiatric Publishing |location=Washington, DC|isbn=9781585628339|oclc=701833161|page=[https://books.google.com/books?id=cJyvBAAAQBAJ&pg=PA87 87]}}</ref>{{rp|page=[https://books.google.com/books?id=0m4MbrnqEWEC&pg=PA44 44]}}<ref name="Kooij-2010"/>

|}

已知「過動」與「衝動」，彼此之間高度相關<ref name="BARKLEY 1989 pp. 203–233"/><ref name="Zhang Wang Cai Yan 2009 pp. 11–15">{{cite journal | last=Zhang | first=Jin-Song | last2=Wang | first2=Yan | last3=Cai | first3=Ru-Gang | last4=Yan | first4=Chong-Huai | title=The brain regulation mechanism of error monitoring in impulsive children with ADHD—An analysis of error related potentials | journal=Neuroscience letters | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=460 | issue=1 | date=2009-08-21 | issn=0304-3940 | pmid=19450665 | doi=10.1016/j.neulet.2009.05.027 | pages=11–15}}</ref><ref name="Aron Dowson Sahakian Robbins 2003 pp. 1465–1468">{{cite journal | last=Aron | first=Adam R | last2=Dowson | first2=Jonathon H | last3=Sahakian | first3=Barbara J | last4=Robbins | first4=Trevor W | title=Methylphenidate improves response inhibition in adults with attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder | journal=Biological Psychiatry | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=54 | issue=12 | year=2003 | issn=0006-3223 | doi=10.1016/s0006-3223(03)00609-7 | pages=1465–1468}}</ref><ref name="Woltering Liu Rokeach Tannock 2013 pp. 1888–1895">{{cite journal | last=Woltering | first=Steven | last2=Liu | first2=Zhongxu | last3=Rokeach | first3=Alan | last4=Tannock | first4=Rosemary | title=Neurophysiological differences in inhibitory control between adults with ADHD and their peers | journal=Neuropsychologia | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=51 | issue=10 | year=2013 | issn=0028-3932 | pmid=23831207 | doi=10.1016/j.neuropsychologia.2013.06.023 | pages=1888–1895}}</ref>。
<!-- {{see also|{{tsl|en|Motor control|運動協調控制}}}}  下方已經有 tsl運動神經控制-->

===衝動性===
{{main article|衝動|延遲的滿足}}

[[FILE:Damon_shocked.jpg|thumb]]）<ref name="Barkley 2012 p. ">{{cite book | last=Barkley | first=Russell | title=Executive functions : what they are, how they work, and why they evolved | publisher=Guilford Press | publication-place=New York | year=2012 | isbn=978-1-4625-0535-7 | oclc=773666263 | page=}}</ref>]]

'''衝動'''是指在[[抑制控制|抑制控制]]上有困難，所以會在尚未深思熟慮前，就開始行動（簡言之，未能謀定而後動）。ADHD往往無法正確判斷什麼是「適當的行為」，這乃是因為ADHD的[[衝動_(心理學)|衝動]]性質反映在[[認知|認知]]上所形成的[[表象|表象]]。由於ADHD的[[自制力|自我抑制能力]]不足，所以往往會不由自主地說出本身不願意說的話或做出本身不願意做的事情或行動。舉例來說：當非ADHD的孩子做出不適當的行為時，只要被老師或家長處罰2到3次就會修正其行為；而ADHD兒童在受到好幾次處罰後，仍持續違反紀律的情形十分普遍。這樣重蹈覆轍的行為不是反抗也不是故意的，而是心裡的衝動所致。具有衝動性特質的人，其[[反应时|反應時間]]（不經深思熟慮的反應），比起同齡或同智能的人要短一些。這種衝動的個性會直接反映在學業上，譬如說，衝動的人傾向在還沒閱讀完較長的題幹，或還沒有讀完全部的答題選項時，就因不耐煩而作答，導致答錯問題的比率甚高。除此之外，曾有個性衝動的人因為沒注意到眼前的障礙物而絆倒，或在沒有注意路況下，就衝到馬路上而發生[[交通事故|交通事故]]的例子。<ref name="社團法人台灣心動家族兒童青少年關懷協會 2012_Definitions">{{cite web | title=ADHD症狀 | website=[[社團法人台灣心動家族兒童青少年關懷協會|社團法人台灣心動家族兒童青少年關懷協會]] | date=2012-11-05 | url=http://www.tc-adhd.com/?page_id=101 | language=zh-tw | access-date=2017-06-22 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160430173911/http://www.tc-adhd.com/?page_id=101 | archivedate=2016-04-30 }}</ref><ref name="Winstanley Eagle Robbins 2006 pp. 379–395">{{cite journal | last=Winstanley | first=Catharine A. | last2=Eagle | first2=Dawn M. | last3=Robbins | first3=Trevor W. | title=Behavioral models of impulsivity in relation to ADHD: Translation between clinical and preclinical studies | journal=Clinical psychology review | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=26 | issue=4 | year=2006 | issn=0272-7358 | pmid=16504359 | pmc=1892795291 | doi=10.1016/j.cpr.2006.01.001 | pages=379–395}}</ref>

一言以蔽之，衝動乃患者經常在「能『立即』獲得酬賞滿足感（Reward）」的點子的驅使下就「立即」行動，行動前沒能{{tsl|en|hindsight||鑑往}}{{tsl|en|foresight||知來}}、縝密思考過行動的緩急輕重、利弊得失、風險及可能帶來的後果，之所以行動幾乎只是為了能『立即』獲得酬賞、回饋、或滿足感（Reward）。
<ref name="ICD-11 reference to impulsivity">{{cite web | title=Mortality and Morbidity Statistics | website=ICD-11 | url=https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f821852937 | access-date=2018-07-21 | quote=Impulsivity is a tendency to act in response to immediate stimuli, without deliberation or consideration of the risks and consequences. | access-date=2018-06-23 | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20180623134621/https://icd.who.int/browse11/l-m/en#/http%3a%2f%2fid.who.int%2ficd%2fentity%2f821852937  | deadurl=no }}</ref><ref name="Robbins Dalley 2017 pp. 81–93">{{cite book | last=Robbins | first=T.W. | last2=Dalley | first2=J.W. | title=Decision Neuroscience | chapter=Impulsivity, Risky Choice, and Impulse Control Disorders | publisher=Elsevier | year=2017 | isbn=978-0-12-805308-9 | doi=10.1016/b978-0-12-805308-9.00007-5 | pages=81–93}}</ref><ref name="Tannock Campbell Seymour Ouellet 2008 pp. 301–351">{{cite book | last=Tannock | first=Rosemary | last2=Campbell | first2=Brian | last3=Seymour | first3=Patricia | last4=Ouellet | first4=Daniele | last5=Soares | first5=Holly | last6=Wang | first6=Paul | last7=Chappell | first7=Phillip | title=Animal and Translational Models for CNS Drug Discovery | chapter=Towards a Biological Understanding of ADHD and the Discovery of Novel Therapeutic Approaches | publisher=Elsevier | year=2008 | isbn=978-0-12-373861-5 | doi=10.1016/b978-0-12-373861-5.00010-2 | pages=301–351 |quote=Impulsivity is broadly defined as “actions without foresight” that are “poorly conceived, prematurely expressed, unduly risky, or inappropriate to the situation, and that often result in undesirable outcomes.}}</ref><ref name="Mestre-Bach Steward Granero Fernández-Aranda 2018 p. ">{{cite journal | last=Mestre-Bach | first=Gemma | last2=Steward | first2=Trevor | last3=Granero | first3=Roser | last4=Fernández-Aranda | first4=Fernando | last5=Talón-Navarro | first5=María Teresa | last6=Cuquerella | first6=Àngel | last7=Baño | first7=Marta | last8=Moragas | first8=Laura | last9=del Pino-Gutiérrez | first9=Amparo | last10=Aymamí | first10=Neus | last11=Gómez-Peña | first11=Mónica | last12=Mallorquí-Bagué | first12=Núria | last13=Vintró-Alcaraz | first13=Cristina | last14=Magaña | first14=Pablo | last15=Menchón | first15=José Manuel | last16=Jiménez-Murcia | first16=Susana | title=Gambling and Impulsivity Traits: A Recipe for Criminal Behavior? | journal=Frontiers in psychiatry | publisher=Frontiers Media SA | volume=9 | date=2018-01-29 | issn=1664-0640 | pmid=29434553 | pmc=5796889 | doi=10.3389/fpsyt.2018.00006 | page=}}</ref><ref name="Horesh Rolnick Iancu Dannon 1997 pp. 92–96">{{cite journal | last=Horesh | first=Neta | last2=Rolnick | first2=Tzipora | last3=Iancu | first3=Iulian | last4=Dannon | first4=Pinhas | last5=Lepkifker | first5=Elie | last6=Apter | first6=Alan | last7=Kotler | first7=Moshe | title=Anger, Impulsivity and Suicide Risk | journal=Psychotherapy and Psychosomatics | publisher=S. == 特徵和症狀 ==
{{main|注意力不足過動症的特質|注意力不足過動症的症狀}}
注意力缺失症患者在學生時期的特徵包含：患者在上課時看起來是靜靜地聽講，但事實上患者對教師所說的內容可能茫然不知、純粹只是望著教師。<ref name="books2000">{{cite book|author=Edward M. Hallowell & John J. Ratey|title=分心不是我的錯（增訂版）：正確診療ADD，重建有計畫的生活方式 Driven to Distraction|url=http://books.google.com/books?id=5OVyCgAAQBAJ|date=2015-09-01|publisher=遠流出版|isbn=978-957-32-7700-2|accessdate=2017-06-27}}</ref>

[[File:Theoretical_delay-of-reinforcement_normal_and_ADHD_gradients.jpg|thumb]]過於延遲的反應（反應包含：緊張、開心等），並造成患者過於不易分辨事情的緩急輕重等症狀。<ref name="Aase Sagvolden 2005 p=12">{{cite journal | last=Aase | first=Heidi | last2=Sagvolden | first2=Terje | journal=Behavioral and Brain Functions | publisher=Springer Nature | volume=1 | issue=1 | year=2005 | issn=1744-9081 | doi=10.1186/1744-9081-1-12 | page=12 | title=Moment-to-moment dynamics of ADHD behaviour}}</ref> <br/>（編註：[[感受|感受力]]、[[感覺|感覺能力]]、[[知覺|感知能力]]）]]

[[File:Proposed_Symptoms_of_ADHD.PNG|thumb]]：過動（Hyperactivity）、缺乏自我抑制（Disinhibition）、健忘（Forgetfulness）、缺乏秩序與組織性（Disorganization）、容易分心（Distractedness）、難以把專注力放對地方（Inattentive）<ref name="Barkley 2012 p. "/>]]

[[File:Dreamy_.jpg|thumb]]是常見於ADHD的{{tsl|en|Personality_type|characteristic|特質}}。<ref> {{cite journal|author=Dr. Tami Steinberg | date=2006 | title= Our day does not end at noon: the expression of Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder outside the school . | journal=Internal Medicine, Behavioral Genetics Clinic | language=he | url=http://makom-m.cet.ac.il/pages/item.asp?s=0&id=-1&defid=103&page=1&item=2983}}</ref><!--Retrieved from:he.wikipedia.org-->]]

注意力不足過動症的主要特徵包括：容易[[遗忘|忘記事情]]、分心、{{tsl|en|Compulsive talking||一說話就停不下來}}、獨佔整個對話交談（monopolizing conversation）、常打斷別人發言<!-- ，且愛[[辯論|辯駁]] --><!--遇到disagreement的時候，溝通討論是好事，因此暫時隱藏這個感覺不太嚴謹的說法。感覺句子的原意是想寫"反嗆"。但在找到嚴謹說法前，暫時隱藏，免得讓人以為多元思考、表達自己的想法是一件壞事。-->、靜不下來、讀寫困難（包括寫錯字，常多一畫或少一畫、拼字錯誤等）、閱讀時會跳行或無法理解文意等，做事易[[延宕|延宕]]，常拖至最後。工作普遍都做不久，{{tsl|en|Racing thoughts|思潮泉湧更迭|持續有點子突然在腦海中蹦出來}}，會一直換工作，顯得三心兩意{{noteTag|name=racing thoughts| 1=報載一名媽媽在洗碗時，腦中想著地板還沒擦，就跑去擦地。過程中又想到家裡沒有衛生紙了，於是趕緊奪門而出......。她想到什麼就做什麼，結果每件家事都只做一半、沒有一樣是完成的。<ref name="Apple Daily">{{cite web | title=孩子常上課分心、撒謊...真的不是故意搗蛋 - 即時新聞 - 20170326 | website=蘋果日報 | date=2017-03-26 | url=http://www.appledaily.com.tw/realtimenews/article/new/20170326/1084790/ | language=zh | access-date=2017-06-26 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170614150219/http://www.appledaily.com.tw/realtimenews/article/new/20170326/1084790/ | archivedate=2017-06-14 }}</ref>}}、缺乏{{tsl|en|Organizing_(structure)||組織}}、[[企劃|規劃]]力，無法把自己想說的話、想做的事具體地表達或規劃出來。逃避需要持續動腦的工作（例如：做家庭作業或學校作業）、無法{{tsl|en|Prioritization|分辨事情的優先次序}}（緩急輕重）、缺乏[[時間管理|時間管理]]的認知。<ref name="Tc_ADHD"/><ref name="autogenerated1">{{cite web |url=http://www.adhd.org.hk/ |title=專注不足/過度活躍症(香港)協會 Hong Kong Association For AD/HD |publisher=Adhd.org.hk |date= |accessdate=2016-12-27 |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20161227061331/http://www.adhd.org.hk/ |archivedate=2016-12-27 }}</ref><ref name="sunshine"/><ref name="UpToDate Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder in adults: Epidemiology, pathogenesis, clinical features, course, assessment, and diagnosis">{{cite web | title=Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder in adults: Epidemiology, pathogenesis, clinical features, course, assessment, and diagnosis | website=UpToDate | url=https://www.uptodate.com/contents/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-in-adults-epidemiology-pathogenesis-clinical-features-course-assessment-and-diagnosis?source=see_link | access-date=2018-07-24 | author=Author:Oscar Bukstein, MD；Section Editor:David Brent, MD；Deputy Editor:Richard Hermann, MD | archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20171029012650/https://www.uptodate.com/contents/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-in-adults-epidemiology-pathogenesis-clinical-features-course-assessment-and-diagnosis?source=see_link | archive-date=2017-10-29 | dead-url=no }}</ref><ref name="Barkley 2012 p. "/>

以上症狀隨患者年齡而有不同表現，譬如說，注意力不足過動症的孩子，其表現通常有：上課不專心、無法抑制自己的衝動以及坐立不安的情況；成人患者的主要問題則常在於無法計劃並完成好他們的[[日常生活|日常生活]]與[[時間表|每日簡單的工作]]<ref name="UpToDate Attention deficit hyperactivity disorder in adults: Epidemiology, pathogenesis, clinical features, course, assessment, and diagnosis"/>。（編註：參見[[成人注意力不足過動症|成人注意力不足過動症]]）

各年齡層的注意力不足過動症患者往往較容易遭遇{{tsl|en|Social competence|社交技巧}}上的問題，例如：[[社交互動|社交互動]]、{{tsl|en|relationship forming|人際關係建立|建立一段人際關係}}及[[人際關係|維持一段人際關係]]等。這個觀察在各注意力不足過動症的三種子類型中都是成立的。大約一半（50%）的患有注意力不足過動症的兒童及青少年曾經歷過来自他人的[[排挤|社交拒絕]]；相形之下，其同儕{{noteTag|name=|1=沒有ADHD的人}}被別人[[社交拒絕|拒絕社交]]的比率約為10-15%<!--原始句子：而其同儕{{noteTag|name=|1=沒有ADHD的人}}遭遇[[社交拒絕|社交上的拒絕]]的比率約為10-15%-->。注意力不足的人比起對照組（非注意力不足過動症患者）更容易遭遇理解他人「{{tsl|en|verbal||口頭}}與[[非言语交际|非口頭]]」言行舉止及交際上的困難，進而對於其社交互動產生負面影響。注意力不足過動症患者也可能在對話的過程中{{tsl|en|Hypnagogia||恍神}}甚至打瞌睡並遺漏他人釋放出的社交暗示。<ref name="V">{{cite journal | last=Coleman | first=WL | title=Social competence and friendship formation in adolescents with attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder. | journal=Adolescent medicine: state of the art reviews | volume=19 | issue=2 | year=2008 | issn=1934-4287 | pmid=18822833 | pages=278–99, x}}</ref>

難以[[憤怒管理|管理憤怒]][[情緒|情緒]]的情況則較常在兒童注意力不足過動症患者身上顯現。<ref name="VI">{{cite web |url=http://www.webmd.com/add-adhd/adhd-anger-management-directory |title=ADHD Anger Management Directory |publisher=Webmd.com |access-date=2014-01-17 |deadurl=no |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20131105032151/http://www.webmd.com/add-adhd/adhd-anger-management-directory |archive-date=2013-11-05  |accessdate=2014-01-17 |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20131105032151/http://www.webmd.com/add-adhd/adhd-anger-management-directory |archivedate=2013-11-05 }}</ref>再者，兒童注意力不足過動症患者通常有{{tsl|en|handwriting|書寫筆跡|寫字}}的困難<ref name="Racine Majnemer Shevell Snider 2008 pp. 399–406">{{cite journal | last=Racine | first=Marie Brossard | last2=Majnemer | first2=Annette | last3=Shevell | first3=Michael | last4=Snider | first4=Laurie | title=Handwriting Performance in Children With Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD) | journal=Journal of child neurology | publisher=SAGE Publications | volume=23 | issue=4 | year=2008 | issn=0883-0738 | pmid=18401033 | doi=10.1177/0883073807309244 | pages=399–406}}</ref><ref name="Capodieci Lachina Cornoldi 2018 pp. 41–49">{{cite journal | last=Capodieci | first=Agnese | last2=Lachina | first2=Simona | last3=Cornoldi | first3=Cesare | title=Handwriting difficulties in children with attention deficit hyperactivity disorder (ADHD) | journal=Research in Developmental Disabilities | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=74 | year=2018 | issn=0891-4222 | doi=10.1016/j.ridd.2018.01.003 | pages=41–49}}</ref>、{{tsl|en|Child_development#growth||言語及行動發展的遲緩}}。雖然這些問題造成患者在現今社會中很大的障礙<ref name="apps.who.int">{{cite web | title=ICD-10 Version:2016 | website=apps.who.int | url=http://apps.who.int/classifications/icd10/browse/2016/en#/F90-F98 | access-date=2018-07-18 | accessdate=2018-04-19 | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170208033519/http://apps.who.int/classifications/icd10/browse/2016/en#/F90-F98 | archivedate=2017-02-08 | deadurl=no }}</ref><ref name="Bellani Moretti Perlini Brambilla 2011 pp. 311–5">{{cite | last=Bellani | first=M | last2=Moretti | first2=A | last3=Perlini | first3=C | last4=Brambilla | first4=P | title=Language disturbances in ADHD. | journal=Epidemiology and psychiatric sciences | volume=20 | issue=4 | year=2011 | issn=2045-7960 | pmid=22201208 | pages=311–5}}</ref>，然而許多注意力不足過動症患者在他們有興趣的事情上都能持續維持專注力，<ref name="Walitza Drechsler Ball 2012 pp. 467–73">{{cite journal | last=Walitza | first=S | last2=Drechsler | first2=R | last3=Ball | first3=J | title="Das schulkind mit ADHS" [The school child with ADHD]. Ther Umsch (in German) | journal=Therapeutische Umschau. Revue therapeutique | volume=69 | issue=8 | year=2012 | issn=0040-5930 | pmid=22851461 | doi=10.1024/0040-5930/a000316 | pages=467–73 | language=de}}</ref>甚至過度專心，成為[[工作狂|工作狂]]。<ref name="找回專注力"/>{{NoteTag|name=|1=ADHD是各類[[成癮|成癮]]的高風險群。<ref name="books2000"/>}}

注意力不足過動症患者遇到需要保持長時間專注的事情，比如說：讀書、寫功課、或{{tsl|en|Reading comprehension|閱讀理解|閱讀}}，就容易出現不適應的情況。<ref name="找回專注力"/>研究結果證實注意力不足過動症本身與低{{tsl|en|Academic_achievement|學業成就}}為直接的因果關係。<ref name="de Zeeuw van Beijsterveldt Ehli de Geus 2017 pp. 278–289">{{cite journal | last=de Zeeuw | first=Eveline L. | last2=van Beijsterveldt | first2=Catharina E. M. | last3=Ehli | first3=Erik A. | last4=de Geus | first4=Eco J. C. | last5=Boomsma | first5=Dorret I. | title=Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder Symptoms and Low Educational Achievement: Evidence Supporting A Causal Hypothesis | journal=Behavior genetics | publisher=Springer Nature | volume=47 | issue=3 | date=2017-02-13 | issn=0001-8244 | pmid=28191586 | pmc=5403868 | doi=10.1007/s10519-017-9836-4 | pages=278–289}}</ref>

不少注意力不足過動症患者（尤其是女性患者）沒有過動症狀，而過去對此症的認識總是集中在過動（多動、過度活躍）症狀上，使得這類「不過動或衝動」的注意力不足過動症患者甚少能被診斷出來。<ref name="pmid19393378">
{{cite journal 
|last1= Emond 
|first1= V 
|last2= Joyal 
|first2= C 
|last3= Poissant |first3= H 
| title= Neuroanatomie structurelle et fonctionnelle du trouble déficitaire d’attention avec ou sans hyperactivité (TDAH) 
|trans-title= Structural and functional neuroanatomy of attention-deficit hyperactivity disorder (ADHD) 
| language=fr
| journal=Encephale 
| volume=35 
| issue=2 
| pages=107–14 
| date= 2009-04
| pmid=19393378 
| doi=10.1016/j.encep.2008.01.005}}</ref><ref name="Singh">
{{cite journal 
|last= Singh 
|first= I 
| title = Beyond polemics: Science and ethics of ADHD 
| journal = Nature Reviews Neuroscience 
| volume = 9 
| issue = 12
| pages = 957–64 
| date =2008-12
| pmid = 19020513 
| doi = 10.1038/nrn2514 }}</ref>

===正向特徵===
<!--敬請確保此節的獨立存在，不要合併到其他章節-->

[[FILE:Photo_opportunity_(513946567).jpg|thumb]]

[[File:Think_different2.png|thumb]]」或是腦海中的想法出現「[[多頭馬車|多頭馬車]]」的原因之一。<ref name="Royce pp. 990–991">{{cite journal | last=Royce | first=J. R. | title=The Nature of Human Intelligence. J. P. Guilford. McGraw-Hill, New York, 1967. xiv + 538 pp., illus. $14.75 | journal=Science | publisher=American Association for the Advancement of Science (AAAS) | volume=162 | issue=3857 | date=1968-11-29 | issn=0036-8075 | doi=10.1126/science.162.3857.990-a | pages=990–991}}</ref><ref name="Oxford University Press">{{cite web | title=Encyclopedia of Psychology | website=Oxford University Press | url=https://global.oup.com/academic/product/encyclopedia-of-psychology-9781557981875 | access-date=2018-12-29}}</ref><ref name="Zhang Wang Cai Yan 2009 pp. 11–15"/><ref name="Abraham Windmann Siefen Daum 2006 pp. 111–123">{{cite journal | last=Abraham | first=Anna | last2=Windmann | first2=Sabine | last3=Siefen | first3=Rainer | last4=Daum | first4=Irene | last5=Güntürkün | first5=Onur | title=Creative Thinking in Adolescents with Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD) | journal=Child neuropsychology : a journal on normal and abnormal development in childhood and adolescence | publisher=Informa UK Limited | volume=12 | issue=2 | year=2006 | issn=0929-7049 | pmid=16754532 | doi=10.1080/09297040500320691 | pages=111–123}}</ref><ref name="White Shah 2011 pp. 673–677">{{cite journal | last=White | first=Holly A. | last2=Shah | first2=Priti | title=Creative style and achievement in adults with attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder | journal=Personality and Individual Differences | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=50 | issue=5 | year=2011 | issn=0191-8869 | doi=10.1016/j.paid.2010.12.015 | pages=673–677}}</ref><ref name="Mayseless Uzefovsky Shalev Ebstein 2013 p. ">{{cite journal | last=Mayseless | first=Naama | last2=Uzefovsky | first2=Florina | last3=Shalev | first3=Idan | last4=Ebstein | first4=Richard P. | last5=Shamay-Tsoory | first5=Simone G. | title=The association between creativity and 7R polymorphism in the dopamine receptor D4 gene (DRD4) | journal=Frontiers in human neuroscience | publisher=Frontiers Media SA | volume=7 | year=2013 | issn=1662-5161 | pmid=23986684 | pmc=3752433 | doi=10.3389/fnhum.2013.00502 | page=}}</ref><ref name="Chakravarty 2010 pp. 606–612">{{cite journal | last=Chakravarty | first=Ambar | title=The creative brain – Revisiting concepts | journal=Medical hypotheses | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=74 | issue=3 | year=2010 | issn=0306-9877 | pmid=19896776 | doi=10.1016/j.mehy.2009.10.014 | pages=606–612}}</ref>]]

注意力不足過動症患者較為正向的特質為：<br>
舉止坦率自然、落落大方、富有[[想像|想像力]]與[[好奇|好奇心]]能夠跳脫框架思考<ref name="super_parenting"/>（編註：參見{{tsl|en|Divergent thinking|發散式思考}}）；思考多元獨特，對直覺較敏感，能深入問題核心發現問題；對自己的想法堅持、特立獨行<ref name="sunshine"/>；具高度[[創造力|創造力]]、追求[[創新|創新]]、[[熱心|熱心]]助人、富有[[正義|正義感]]和[[幽默|幽默感]]、活潑開朗<ref name="找回專注力"/>；勇於[[冒險|冒險]]、韌性十足、源源不絕的活力<ref name="Archer 2015 p. "/>。有[[興趣|興趣]]時非常能夠堅持<ref name="super_parenting">{{cite book|author1=Edward M. Hallowell|author2=Peter S. Jensen|title=分心就該這樣教 從優勢能力出發，找出學習新方向|url=http://books.google.com/books?id=5fW2AAAAQBAJ&pg=PP24|date=2009-11-01|publisher=遠流出版|isbn=978-957-32-6544-3|pages=24–}}</ref>、具備[[批判性思维|批判性思维]]。<ref name="webmd.com">{{cite web |url=http://www.webmd.com/add-adhd/features/positives |title=Is There a Positive Side to Adult ADHD? |author =Eric Metcalf, MPH |publisher=WebMD, LLC |accessdate=August 17, 2015 | archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181225054830/https://www.webmd.com/add-adhd/positives#2 | archive-date=2018-12-25 | access-date=2018-12-25}}</ref><ref name="sunshine">{{cite web|author1=哈洛威爾|title=淺談ＡＤＤ注意力缺失症|url=http://www.mdnkids.com.tw/specialeducation/detail.asp?sn=450|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20161005160532/http://www.mdnkids.com.tw/specialeducation/detail.asp?sn=450|archivedate=2016-10-05|website=國語日報社|accessdate=2016-10-05|language=zh-tw}}</ref><ref name="Archer 2015 p. ">{{cite book | last=Archer | first=Dale | title=The ADHD advantage : what you thought was a diagnosis may be your greatest strength | publisher=Avery | publication-place=New York, New York | year=2015 | isbn=978-0-399-57345-3 | page= | url=https://www.amazon.com/ADHD-Advantage-Diagnosis-Greatest-Strength/dp/0399573453 | access-date=2017-06-24 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170224052344/https://www.amazon.com/ADHD-Advantage-Diagnosis-Greatest-Strength/dp/0399573453 | archivedate=2017-02-24 }}</ref><ref name="Royce pp. 990–991"/><ref name="Oxford University Press"/><ref name="Zhang Wang Cai Yan 2009 pp. 11–15"/><ref name="Abraham Windmann Siefen Daum 2006 pp. 111–123"/><ref name="White Shah 2011 pp. 673–677"/><ref name="Mayseless Uzefovsky Shalev Ebstein 2013 p. "/><ref name="Chakravarty 2010 pp. 606–612"/><ref name="Hufar Friday 2002"/>

<!-- === 人際交往與互動 === 暫時註解，因為人際交往在段落一開始就提到了 --> 

===婚姻關係===
{{see also2|{{tsl|en|Procrastination#Negative impact|拖延對ADHD的情感關係造成的影響}}|[[成人注意力不足過動症#婚姻等親密關係|成人注意力不足過動症§婚姻等親密關係]]}}
台灣精神科醫師[[高淑芬|高淑芬]]在《找回專注力：成人ADHD全方位自助手冊》一書中指出，ADHD患者活潑開朗、熱心助人、說話風趣、勇於[[表白|告白]]的特性對於兩性交往與[[婚姻|婚姻]]來說都具有加分作用；但交往一段時間後，ADHD患者的負面特質，例如：沒[[耐心|耐心]]、容易遲到、無法專心聽人說話、交代的事情老是忘記、需要幫忙的時候找不到人、[[習慣|生活習慣]]及生活作息不正常、及{{tsl|en|Absent-mindedness||個性迷糊}}等，就可能讓對方萌生退意。<ref name="找回專注力"/>高淑芬亦指出，如果順利交往、結婚，則接下來注意力不足過動症患者可能遇到的挑戰為：比起交往時期多了許多日常生活之事，患者可能會因為忘記付帳單、照顧小孩很散漫、做事有始無終而引起夫妻間的爭吵，為婚姻生活埋下陰影。<ref name="找回專注力"/><ref name="ADHD relationship">{{cite web | last=ADHD | first=CHADD – The National Resource on ADHD | title=Marriage and Partnerships - CHADD | website=CHADD - The National Resource on ADHD | url=http://www.help4adhd.org/Understanding-ADHD/For-Adults/Living-with-ADHD-A-Lifespan-Disorder/Relationships-Social-Skills/Marriage-and-Partnerships.aspx | access-date=2018-06-14 | deadurl=no | archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20171023142355/http://help4adhd.org/Understanding-ADHD/For-Adults/Living-with-ADHD-A-Lifespan-Disorder/Relationships-Social-Skills/Marriage-and-Partnerships.aspx | archivedate=2017-10-23 }}</ref>

然而，高淑芬強調，只要ADHD患者可以提升專注力並且落實執行力，一樣可以如同其他人。<ref name="找回專注力"/>

===智力===
注意力不足過動症患者的[[智力|智力]]與[[潛能|潛力]]和非注意力不足過動症患者相仿，然而因為注意力不足過動症的症狀，使得其[[智力測驗|智力測驗]]結果可能產生較大的誤差<ref name="Frazier Demaree Youngstrom 2004 pp. 543–555">{{cite journal | last=Frazier | first=Thomas W. | last2=Demaree | first2=Heath A. | last3=Youngstrom | first3=Eric A. | title=Meta-Analysis of Intellectual and Neuropsychological Test Performance in Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder. | journal=Neuropsychology | publisher=American Psychological Association (APA) | volume=18 | issue=3 | year=2004 | issn=1931-1559 | pmid=15291732 | doi=10.1037/0894-4105.18.3.543 | pages=543–555}}</ref><ref name="Mackenzie Wonders 2016 p. ">{{cite journal | last=Mackenzie | first=Genevieve B. | last2=Wonders | first2=Elif | title=Rethinking Intelligence Quotient Exclusion Criteria Practices in the Study of Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder | journal=Frontiers in psychology | publisher=Frontiers Media SA | volume=7 | date=2016-05-31 | issn=1664-1078 | pmid=27303350 | pmc=4886698 | doi=10.3389/fpsyg.2016.00794 | page=}}</ref>。

由於ADHD可能被當成[[學習障礙|學習障礙]]或[[智能障礙|智能障礙]]為主的方式處理，因此文獻指出，面對兒童青少年和成人之學習障礙或智能障礙患者的相關人員應具備ADHD的專業知識<ref name="Ahuja Martin Langley Thapar 2013 pp. 890–895.e1">{{cite journal | last=Ahuja | first=Alka | last2=Martin | first2=Joanna | last3=Langley | first3=Kate | last4=Thapar | first4=Anita | title=Intellectual Disability in Children with Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder | journal=The Journal of Pediatrics | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=163 | issue=3 | year=2013 | issn=0022-3476 | pmid=23608559 | pmc=4078221 | doi=10.1016/j.jpeds.2013.02.043 | pages=890–895.e1}}</ref><ref name="Goldman p=1100">{{cite journal | last=Goldman | first=Larry S. | title=Diagnosis and Treatment of Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder in Children and Adolescents | journal=JAMA | publisher=American Medical Association (AMA) | volume=279 | issue=14 | date=1998-04-08 | issn=0098-7484 | doi=10.1001/jama.279.14.1100 | page=1100}}</ref>。

台灣醫師高淑芬在其著作中提到，若能在大約九、十歲以前把握年齡較小、症狀較為單純時治療，可以避免往後病情複雜化（衍生共病）。再者，能在早期建立良好的學習及生活習慣，培養自信心及責任感，對注意力不足過動症患者的未來將有深遠的影響<ref name="衛生福利部 注意力不足過動症"/><ref name="找回專注力"/><ref name="幫助ADHD孩子快樂成長">{{cite book|author=高淑芬 |title=家有過動兒：幫助ADHD孩子快樂成長 |publisher=心靈工坊 |location=台北 |isbn=9789866112805 |date=2013-08-28 |accessdate=2016-12-09|url= }}</ref>。

=== 可能與注意力不足過動症有關的疾病 ===
<!--附上原始版本對照：在兒童注意力不足過動症患者中，大約有<big><big>⅔</big></big>的機率伴隨其他與注意力不足過動症有關的特徵或疾病。常見的特徵或共病如下：-->
在<!--兒童-->注意力不足過動症患者中，大約會有<!--原始版本：三分之二-->{{frac|2|3}} 的機率伴隨其他有關的特徵或疾病<ref name="pmid22851461"/>。常見的特徵或共病如下：

* 在20%至30%的注意力不足過動症患者中，觀察到有[[學習障礙|特殊學習需求]]（舊稱學習障礙、學習困難）<!--附上原始版本對照： [[學習障礙|特殊學習需求]]（舊稱學習障礙、學習困難）在20%~30%的注意力不足過動症患者中被觀察到 --><ref name="Walitza Drechsler Ball 2012 pp. 467–73 II">{{cite journal | last=Walitza | first=S | last2=Drechsler | first2=R | last3=Ball | first3=J | title=[The school child with ADHD]. | journal=Therapeutische Umschau. Revue therapeutique | volume=69 | issue=8 | year=2012 | issn=0040-5930 | pmid=22851461 | doi=10.1024/0040-5930/a000316 | pages=467–73 | language=de}}</ref>。言語發展遲緩及學習技巧的困難皆涵蓋在學習障礙的範疇中。然而注意力不足過動症本身並不包含在學習障礙中，只不過注意力不足過動症仍經常造成學業上的困難。<ref name=BaileyHC>{{cite web
 |last        = Bailey
 |first       = Eileen
 |title       = ADHD and Learning Disabilities: How can you help your child cope with ADHD and subsequent Learning Difficulties? There is a way.
 |url         = http://www.healthcentral.com/adhd/education-159625-5.html
 |publisher   = Remedy Health Media, LLC.
 |access-date = 2013-11-15
 |deadurl     = no
 |archiveurl  = https://web.archive.org/web/20131203092339/http://www.healthcentral.com/adhd/education-159625-5.html
 |archivedate = 2013-12-03
}}</ref>
* [[妥瑞氏症|妥瑞氏症]]。<ref name="nhs.uk 2018"/>
* [[癲癇|癲癇]]。<ref name="nhs.uk 2018"/>
* [[對立反抗症|對立反抗症]]以及[[行為規範障礙|行為規範障礙]]：這兩個疾病通常有著[[反社會|反社會]]的特徵{{noteTag|name=|1=「對立反抗症」、「行為規範障礙」、「反社會」既不等同「獨立思考能力」與「批判能力」也不是「判斷能力」}}<!--（但不應與具備獨立思考的批判能力相混淆）-->，例如：抱持只要我喜歡，有什麼不可以的心態且{{tsl|en|stubborn||固執}}、[[侵略_(社會科學)|帶有攻擊性的（防禦心強）]]、經常突然暴怒（Short-tempered）{{noteTag|name=|1=憤怒管理與衝動控制相關，憤怒及衝動管理能力不足將有較高可能在一時的衝動及憤怒驅使之下做出攻擊行為（impulsive aggression）<ref name="JENSEN YOUNGSTROM STEINER FINDLING 2007 pp. 309–322"/><ref name="Saylor Amann 2016 pp. 19–25"/>}}、{{tsl|en|temper tantrums||鬧脾氣}}、言行隱晦（deceitfulness）、[[說謊|說謊]]、和[[偷竊|偷竊]]等。<ref name="XI">{{cite web
 |location    = USA
 |url         = https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/19940426

 |archiveurl  = https://web.archive.org/web/20161129022121/https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/19940426

*{{tsl|en|Intermittent explosive disorder|間歇性暴怒症}}<ref name=DSM5 />
* [[焦慮症|焦慮症]]越來越頻繁地在注意力不足過動症患者身上觀察到。<ref name="autogenerated3">{{cite

|PMID=20861593}}
{{open access}}</ref><ref name="the sixth citation">{{ cite journal| author=Yin-To Liao, Pei-Chin Lee, Nien-Che Hung, Shu-Hsin Lee, Jun-Cheng Weng, Vincent Chin-Hung Chen*. | title=Association Between Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder Symptoms and Bulimia. |journal =Taiwanese J Psychiatry |date= 2015 Jun | volume=29 | issue=2 | page=98-108 | url=https://www.researchgate.net/publication/279045845_Association_between_Attention_Deficit_Hyperactivity_Disorder_Symptoms_and_Bulimia_among_College_Students }}</ref>
* [[不寧腿症|不寧腿症]]在注意力不足過動症患者身上觀察到的次數越來越頻繁。此症大多由[[缺鐵性貧血|缺鐵性貧血]]造成。然而，不寧腿也可能單純僅是注意力不足過動症的一部份。不寧腿症的確診需要經過仔細的診斷以與注意力不足過動症區分（細節可再參閱[[人類鐵代謝|人類鐵代謝]]、{{tsl|en|Hypoxemia|血氧不足}}）。<ref name="XII">

 |url         = https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/21365608

* [[強迫症|強迫症]]可能與注意力不足過動症併發，且兩者有著許多相同的特徵。<ref name="Krull, KR">{{cite web
 |url          = http://www.uptodate.com/contents/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-in-children-and-adolescents-clinical-features-and-diagnosis#5
 |title        = "Evaluation and diagnosis of attention deficit hyperactivity disorder in children".
 |subscription = yes
 |publisher    = [[UpToDate|UpToDate]] & Wolters Kluwer Health
 |author       = Krull, KR
 |website      = Uptodate.com
 |date         = 5 December 2007.
 |accessdate   = 2016-12-09
 |deadurl      = no
 |archiveurl   = https://web.archive.org/web/20161129025720/http://www.uptodate.com/contents/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-in-children-and-adolescents-clinical-features-and-diagnosis#5
 |archivedate  = 2016-11-29
}}</ref>強迫症的症狀也可能是ADHD患者後天發展出的{{tsl|en|Coping_(psychology)|處理 (心理學)|應對方法}}，用以彌補其ADHD的症狀所致。<ref name="Brown Katz Roth Beers 2014 pp. 131–136">{{cite journal | last=Brown | first=Franklin C. | last2=Katz | first2=Lynda J. | last3=Roth | first3=Robert M. | last4=Beers | first4=Sue R. | title=The relationship of self-reported subclinical obsessive-compulsive symptoms and impulsivity among adults with AD/HD | journal=Psychiatry research | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=216 | issue=1 | date=2014-04-30 | issn=0165-1781 | pmid=24556290 | doi=10.1016/j.psychres.2014.01.034 | pages=131–136}}</ref>
*{{tsl|en|Stereotypic movement disorder|刻板的慣性動作症}}<ref name=DSM5 />
* [[嗜睡症|嗜睡症]]或[[猝睡症|猝睡症]]的患者通常有著專注力上的不足且難以保持醒著的狀態。此症患者通常會在座位上晃動、打哈欠發出聲音、伸展等明顯藉由過動來維繫{{tsl|en|arousal||精神}}與{{tsl|en|Alertness||警覺}}。<ref name="Krull, KR"/>
* 睡眠障礙常與注意力不足過動症共伴出現。睡眠障礙症候群也可能是注意力不足過動症用藥的副作用。在兒童注意力不足過動症患者中，[[失眠|失眠]]是最常見的睡眠障礙症狀，也是行為治療中較為優先的治療項目。 難以入眠的情況是注意力不足過動症患者們最常面臨的問題。然而，注意力不足過動症患者們也常常是深層（度）睡眠者，且有難以在上午起床的狀況。[[褪黑素|褪黑激素]]有時用來治療有難以入睡問題的注意力不足過動症患童。<ref name=Owens2008>{{cite journal 
| author = Owens JA 
| title = Sleep disorders and attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder

* 注意力不足過動症患者相較於<!--疑似贅字：其他-->非注意力不足過動症患者，有著較高的[[夜遺尿|夜遺尿]]風險。<ref name="XX">{{cite web

* [[情緒障礙|情感性疾患]]：特別是[[雙極性症候群|雙極性症候群]]以及[[重性抑郁障碍|重性抑郁障碍]]<ref name="autogenerated3"/><ref name="3rd Liang Yang Kuo Liao 2018 pp. 96–105">{{cite journal | last=Liang | first=Sophie Hsin-Yi | last2=Yang | first2=Yao-Hsu | last3=Kuo | first3=Ting-Yu | last4=Liao | first4=Yin-To | last5=Lin | first5=Tzu-Chin | last6=Lee | first6=Yena | last7=McIntyre | first7=Roger S. | last8=Kelsen | first8=Brent A. | last9=Wang | first9=Tsu-Nai | last10=Chen | first10=Vincent Chin-Hung | title=Suicide risk reduction in youths with attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder prescribed methylphenidate: A Taiwan nationwide population-based cohort study | journal=Research in Developmental Disabilities | publisher=Elsevier BV | volume=72 | year=2018 | issn=0891-4222 | doi=10.1016/j.ridd.2017.10.023 | pages=96–105}}</ref>。同時帶有「過動-衝動、分心」的男性ADHD，有較高的機率衍生出[[情感障礙|情感障礙]]為共病。<ref name="Wilens-2010">{{cite journal 
|vauthors=Wilens TE, Spencer TJ 
| title = Understanding attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder from childhood to adulthood 
| journal = Postgrad Med 
| volume = 122 
| issue = 5 
| pages = 97–109 
| date = 2010-09
|  pmid = 20861593 
| pmc = 3724232 
| doi = 10.3810/pgm.2010.09.2206 }}</ref>18歲左右或已滿18歲的ADHD患者有時也會出現躁鬱症，因此醫療人員必須謹慎地做出診斷以確保該患者罹患的ADHD和躁鬱症都能獲得妥善治療。<ref name="pmid21717696">{{cite journal |vauthors=Baud P, Perroud N, Aubry JM |title=[Bipolar disorder and attention deficit/hyperactivity disorder in adults: differential diagnosis or comorbidity] |language=fr |journal=Rev Med Suisse |volume=7 |issue=297 |pages=1219–1222 |date=June 2011 |pmid=21717696 }}</ref>
* {{tsl|en|Sluggish cognitive tempo||遲緩的認知速率}}（SCT）：是一個存在於早期的疾病名稱。SCT的症狀與ADHD幾乎完全相同，約有30–50%符合SCT診斷的人也符合ADHD的診斷。<ref name="Barkley, R. A. 2014">{{cite journal|first=R. A.|year=2014|title=Sluggish Cognitive Tempo (Concentration Deficit Disorder?): Current Status, Future Directions, and a Plea to Change the Name|url=https://psychology.uiowa.edu/sites/psychology.uiowa.edu/files/groups/nikolas/files/Barkley,%202014.pdf|journal=Journal of Abnormal Child Psychology|volume=42|issue=|pages=117–125|doi=10.1007/s10802-013-9824-y|pmid=24234590|via=|author=Barkley|deadurl=no|archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20170809102631/https://psychology.uiowa.edu/sites/psychology.uiowa.edu/files/groups/nikolas/files/Barkley%2C%202014.pdf|archivedate=2017-08-09}}</ref>
* [[物質濫用症候群|物質濫用症候群]]：青少年與成人注意力不足過動症患者皆有相較對照組<!--疑似贅字：較-->高的物質濫用風險。物質濫用的原因之一可能是腦中原有的{{tsl|en|reward pathway||回饋酬賞迴路/路徑}}因各種因素而由另一事物所觸發的「回饋酬賞迴路/路徑」取代<ref name="Kooij-2010"/>。ADHD合併物質濫用的患者中，最常濫用的物質為[[酒精|酒]]和[[大麻|藥用大麻]]<ref name="Kooij-2010">{{cite journal |last1= Kooij |first1= SJ |last2= Bejerot |first2= S |last3= Blackwell |first3= A |last4= Caci |first4= H |last5= Casas-Brugué |first5= M |last6= Carpentier |first6= PJ |last7= Edvinsson |first7= D |last8= Fayyad |first8= J |last9= Foeken |first9= K |last10= Fitzgerald |first10= M |last11= Gaillac |first11= V |last12= Ginsberg |first12= Y |last13= Henry |first13= C |last14= Krause |first14= J |last15= Lensing |first15= MB |last16= Manor |first16= I |last17= Niederhofer |first17= H |last18= Nunes-Filipe |first18= C |last19= Ohlmeier |first19= MD |last20= Oswald |first20= P |last21= Pallanti |first21= S |last22= Pehlivanidis |first22= A |last23= Ramos-Quiroga |first23= JA |last24= Rastam |first24= M |last25= Ryffel-Rawak |first25= D |last26= Stes |first26= S |last27= Asherson |first27= P |displayauthors= 4 | title = European consensus statement on diagnosis and treatment of adult ADHD: The European Network Adult ADHD | journal = BMC Psychiatry | volume = 10 | issue = | pages = 67 | year = 2010 | pmid = 20815868 | pmc = 2942810 | doi = 10.1186/1471-244X-10-67 }}</ref><ref name="4th Liao Chen Ng Huang 2017 pp. 26–33">{{cite journal | last=Liao | first=Yin-To | last2=Chen | first2=Chi-Yen | last3=Ng | first3=Mei-Hing | last4=Huang | first4=Kuo-You | last5=Shao | first5=Wen-Chuan | last6=Lin | first6=Tsang-Yaw | last7=Chen | first7=Vincent Chin-Hung | last8=Gossop | first8=Michael | title=Depression and severity of substance dependence among heroin dependent patients with ADHD symptoms | journal=The American journal on addictions | publisher=Wiley | volume=26 | issue=1 | date=2016-12-20 | year=2017 | issn=1055-0496 | pmid=27997065 | doi=10.1111/ajad.12487 | pages=26–33}}</ref>一旦ADHD合併物質濫用，ADHD的治療會變得更加困難。如果ADHD合併「嚴重的」物質濫用問題，基於往後衍生的風險大小之考量，物質濫用問題將被優先治療。<ref name=NICE2009-part2>{{cite book |title=Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder: Diagnosis and Management of ADHD in Children, Young People and Adults |author=National Collaborating Centre for Mental Health |series=NICE Clinical Guidelines |volume=72 |publisher=British Psychological Society |location=Leicester |isbn=978-1-85433-471-8 |date=2009 |url=https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/books/NBK53652/ |chapter=Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder |pages=[https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/books/NBK53663/#ch2.s8 18–26], [https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/books/NBK53663/#ch2.s41 38] |chapter-url=https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/books/NBK53663/ |via=NCBI Bookshelf |deadurl=no |archiveurl=https://web.archive.org/web/20160113133612/http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/books/NBK53652/ |archivedate=2016-01-13 }}</ref><ref name="Wilens-2011">{{cite journal |vauthors=Wilens TE, Morrison NR | title = The intersection of attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder and substance abuse | journal = Curr Opin Psychiatry | volume = 24 | issue = 4 | pages = 280–285 | date = July 2011 | pmid = 21483267 | pmc = 3435098 | doi = 10.1097/YCO.0b013e328345c956}}</ref>{{noteTag|name=|1=合併物持成癮的ADHD患者將有較高機率罹患[[性病|性病]]。<ref name="Chen Hsu Huang Bai 2018 pp. 48–53">{{cite journal | last=Chen | first=Mu-Hong | last2=Hsu | first2=Ju-Wei | last3=Huang | first3=Kai-Lin | last4=Bai | first4=Ya-Mei | last5=Ko | first5=Nai-Ying | last6=Su | first6=Tung-Ping | last7=Li | first7=Cheng-Ta | last8=Lin | first8=Wei-Chen | last9=Tsai | first9=Shih-Jen | last10=Pan | first10=Tai-Long | last11=Chang | first11=Wen-Han | last12=Chen | first12=Tzeng-Ji | title=Sexually
